My initial thought was Volk won 3-2 or 4-1.  Islam won rd 1 - Volk rocks Islam back into the cage however Islam dropped Volk to a knee, landed the harder shots, outstruck him on the feet, and took his back for a good portion of the rd. Clearly Islam  Volk won rd 2 - dropped Islam, landed the harder shots, & neutralized the wrestling. Volk & Islam both threw knees. Volk landed BIG knee which busted Islam's nose open & could've KOed him. Islam threw a medium degree knee which Volk dipped into however it only caused bruises due to the way he threw it and how Volk dipped into it. Islam rocks Volk backward, Islam outlands Volk on the feet, lands hard shots in pocket but so does Volk, Volk outlands him in the clinch, competitive rd but clearly Volk.   Volk won rd 3 - Volk neutralized wrestling, Islam took Volk's back for 5 secs, Volk neutralizes wrestling again, outlands Islam in clinch, Volk throws 3 bombs in clinch; one landed and it was the last shot: biggest shot of the rd by far: which also landed flush in clinch & somehow didn't KO, or even wobble Islam, Volk damn near takes Islam down, Islam with good balance; gets up, Volk runs face first into Islam's medium-hard snipe shot; opens a small cut on him, Volk slightly outstruck Islam in strikes on the feet around 8-7 in strikes btw there was a hard leg kick Islam threw which Volk checked I counted it as a strike for Volk, Volk landed the harder shots, due to the cut being minor unlike the bloody nose Volk gave Islam & the impact Volk had on it, with this shot not being as hard, & all the other things Volk did in this rd, Volk takes it.  Volk won rd 4 - Volk was outlanding him on the feet 5-3 in strikes, Islam perfectly times takedown on Volk almost like a robot, & takes his back for like 3 mins mostly taking unanswered shots & not rlly doing anything effective with the attempt. Most of those unanswered shots were a lot of medium, & a lot big shots. Islam landing medium shots for the most part.  Volk won rd 5 - Islam threw 3 big knees 1. Volk dipped into again, the other 2 in clinch with the last cutting him open which were all big shots. This cut being the worst cut of the fight. Volk neutralizes wrestling immediately after being took down, Islam outstruck Volk, Neutralizes wrestling after Islam shoots again, Volk dropped Islam bad, & finished strong by landing nice, hard G&P & along with good offensive wrestling as well. Now listen closely, Islam did land 3 knees, 2 of them being big af, 1 of them delivering the worst cut of the fight. However that dmg Islam took on the ground gave Islam a rlly bad black eye with a cut underneath, & bruises practically all over his face; all in that round from the G&P & again, when Volk dropped him; smth could've got swollen from that too. 5th was the closest by far, closer than I thought it was. I saw a lot of stuff I didn't see the first time in this fight. I watched the fight like 3-4 times 2-3 times in slow-mo, Volk won. Meaning Volk landed the harder shots. If Volk didn't drop Islam in that 5th rd I would be giving Islam the rd but like I said, he not only dropped him, he did all that to his face in that rd.
